*Selection Criteria*:
1. Problem statement given by the team should be innovative.

  *आपणांस व आपल्या परिवारास दीपावली च्या हार्दिक शुभेच्छा. हि दीपावली आपणांस सुखाची, समाधानाची, भरभराटीची, आनंदाची, आरोग्य दायी जावो हीच  महालक्ष्मी चरणी प्रार्थना*
🚩🚩🚩🚩🚩
।। अथ श्री-सूक्त मंत्र पाठ ।।

1- ॐ हिरण्यवर्णां हरिणीं, सुवर्णरजतस्त्रजाम् ।
चन्द्रां हिरण्मयीं लक्ष्मीं, जातवेदो म आ वह ।।

2- तां म आ वह जातवेदो, लक्ष्मीमनपगामिनीम् ।
यस्यां हिरण्यं विन्देयं, गामश्वं पुरूषानहम् ।।

3- अश्वपूर्वां रथमध्यां, हस्तिनादप्रमोदिनीम् ।
श्रियं देवीमुप ह्वये, श्रीर्मा देवी जुषताम् ।।

4- कां सोस्मितां हिरण्यप्राकारामार्द्रां ज्वलन्तीं तृप्तां तर्पयन्तीम् ।
पद्मेस्थितां पद्मवर्णां तामिहोप ह्वये श्रियम् ।।

5- चन्द्रां प्रभासां यशसा ज्वलन्तीं श्रियं लोके देवजुष्टामुदाराम् ।
तां पद्मिनीमीं शरणं प्र पद्ये अलक्ष्मीर्मे नश्यतां त्वां वृणे ।।

6- आदित्यवर्णे तपसोऽधि जातो वनस्पतिस्तव वृक्षोऽक्ष बिल्वः ।
तस्य फलानि तपसा नुदन्तु या अन्तरा याश्च बाह्या अलक्ष्मीः ।।

7- उपैतु मां दैवसखः, कीर्तिश्च मणिना सह ।
प्रादुर्भूतोऽस्मि राष्ट्रेऽस्मिन्, कीर्तिमृद्धिं ददातु मे ।।

8- क्षुत्पिपासामलां ज्येष्ठामलक्ष्मीं नाशयाम्यहम् ।
अभूतिमसमृद्धिं च, सर्वां निर्णुद मे गृहात् ।।

9- गन्धद्वारां दुराधर्षां, नित्यपुष्टां करीषिणीम् ।
ईश्वरीं सर्वभूतानां, तामिहोप ह्वये श्रियम् ।।

10- मनसः काममाकूतिं, वाचः सत्यमशीमहि ।
पशूनां रूपमन्नस्य, मयि श्रीः श्रयतां यशः ।।

11- कर्दमेन प्रजा भूता मयि सम्भव कर्दम ।
श्रियं वासय मे कुले मातरं पद्ममालिनीम् ।।

12- आपः सृजन्तु स्निग्धानि चिक्लीत वस मे गृहे ।
नि च देवीं मातरं श्रियं वासय मे कुले ।।

13- आर्द्रां पुष्करिणीं पुष्टिं पिंगलां पद्ममालिनीम् ।
चन्द्रां हिरण्मयीं लक्ष्मीं, जातवेदो म आ वह ।।

14- आर्द्रां य करिणीं यष्टिं सुवर्णां हेममालिनीम् ।
सूर्यां हिरण्मयीं लक्ष्मीं जातवेदो म आ वह ।।

15- तां म आ वह जातवेदो लक्ष्मीमनपगामिनीम् ।
यस्यां हिरण्यं प्रभूतं गावो दास्योऽश्वान् विन्देयं पुरुषानहम् ।।

16- य: शुचि: प्रयतो भूत्वा जुहुयादाज्यमन्वहम् ।
सूक्तं पंचदशर्चं च श्रीकाम: सततं जपेत् ।।
।। इति समाप्ति ।।

11/24/22, 23:08 - Prof. Dr Uday Patka(HOD): The grand inaugration of UNESCO INDIA-AFRICA Hackathon 2022 was done by Hon'ble Chief Minister Adityanath Yogi. 
Our theme was drinking water and sanitation and in this problem statement was Aquifer Mapping and Management of Ground Water Resources. 
36 hours of hackathon it was, at night while hackathon was going on our Chief Executive Officer (Abhay Jhere) came, met us and took a picture with us. 
The journey of the Hackathon was amazing I enjoyed a lot and learnt new things. It was a great experience with the African students. Some of the African students were unable to understand English, we guys were facing difficulty in communicating with them so, we used Google Translator for communication. But still the African students gave their best 👍 and they all are happy because they all have got chance to visit India. 
The Inaugration of this hackathon was amazing. All participating students represented their country by wearing their traditional dresses. 
The entire journey of this International Hackathon was overwhelming.

11/29/22, 14:07 - Prof. Dr Uday Patka(HOD): *IET Pune LN*
 
*Presentation Competition*

*“IdeaIn10 (2022)-Pune Region”*
 
 
We are happy to inform you that the IET Pune LN’s presentation competition “IdeaIn10 (2022) - Pune Region”  will be organized at MIT-WPU Campus, Kothrud, Pune. The “IdeaIn10 (2022) - Pune Region” competition is open for the students of Engineering and Technology, graduates and young professionals from Pune Region, aged 18 – 30 years. This competition will provide a platform to young minds to explore and showcase their presentation and technical skills. 

*Details for participation in “IdeaIn10 (2022) - Pune Region” competition*
*Date of Competition*: 10th December 2022
*Time*: 10:00 am onwards
*Venue*: Second Floor, Dhruv Building, Faculty of Engineering & Technology, MIT WPU Campus, Kothrud, Pune 

*Registration Link*: https://forms.gle/ZXxJNphuL54uUEMt7 

*Eligibility Criteria: Engineering students, recent graduates, apprentices and young professionals from Pune region, aged 18 to 30 years can participate.

*Note* 
*Registration is compulsory
*Last date of Registration is 5th December 2022.


*Briefing notes for competitors*
This Competition is organized by IET Pune Local Network 
Present the technical topic (subject related to Engineering and Technology) for 10 mins
Presentation on Final year project having societal or industry relevance is also acceptable
Competitors should provide a brief synopsis of their presentation (100-200 words) as a hard copy during presentation
Competitors should carry their presentation in Pen drive, and have to upload on the system at the venue before the session starts
*The prizes are: Certificate and prize money to winner and Runner up of Rs. 14000/- and Rs. 9000/- respectively and participation certificate to all other participants*

Warm Regards,
Coordinator: Dr. Vitthal S. Gutte (9422274784, vitthal.gutte@mitwpu.edu.in )

I am writing to you to inform you and request to spread the word to your previous students about a JRF position in a sponsored project with me.
The title of this project is “LoRa-WSN- based IoT Communication Platform for Precision Agriculture” funded by Technology-Innovation Hub (TIH), IIT Bombay.
This project aims to develop a communication platform using the LoRa protocol
for precision agriculture applications.

12/16/22, 16:13 - Prof. Dr Uday Patka(HOD): PM-YUVA Mentorship Scheme 2.0 has been launched by the Ministry of Education, Government of lndia to train young and budding authors (below 30 years of age) for the year 2022-23 through the National Book Trust, lndia as the implementing Agency.
The Theme of PM-YUVA 2.0 is Democracy (institutions, Events, People, and Constitutional Values). The scheme will help to develop a stream of writers who can write on various facets of Democracy in lndia encompassing the past, present and future.
An online National Contest is being organized from 2nd October 2022 - 15th January 2023 to select the authors under the Scheme. There is a provision for payment of a Scholarship of Rs. 50,000 per month for a period of six months to be paid to each of the selected 75 authors. National Book Trust, lndia will be publishing the books produced by the young authors as part of the Mentorship Scheme.
You are requested to encourage the students for participation in this prestigious scheme. The details can be accessed at www.nbtindia.gov.in and at https://www.mygov.in 
Please find below the link to the Contest and other details for ready reference 
https://innovateindia.mygov.in/yuva/

12/16/22, 16:14 - Prof. Dr Uday Patka(HOD): Greetings of the day..

We hope this email finds you in the best of spirits in these tough times.

We are happy to inform you that the Government of India has taken up various initiatives for the upliftment of Scheduled Castes (SCs), Scheduled Tribes (STs), Women and Economically Weaker Section (EWS) in the country. This includes scholarships, Free Coaching, Economic empowerment schemes and related activities. As the efforts in this direction is significant for upliftment of various sections of the society, there is a need to provide adequate opportunity for candidates to gain expertise and skills in Information Technology, Electronics and related domains which are expected to be leveraged in near future.

Considering these aspects Work Based Learning (WBL) programme in Niche/Emerging Technologies is a unique initiative to provide employability skills to the individuals of SC, ST, Women and EWS.

The Key Features of the WBL:

This programme will provide an opportunity to selected SC/ST/EWS/Women candidates to acquire Technical Knowledge Expansion; Real-time Working Skills; Technology Use; Problem Solving Skills; Reasoning; Ideation; Analytical Thinking; Interpersonal Skills, etc. in a professional work environment. This programme would aim to achieve the following: 

It facilitates SC/ ST/ EWS/ Women candidates for transition from college environment to the corporate world, and thereby provides them with a real-time exposure on niche technological project/ activity in organizations under MeitY.
The Programme provides direct practical experience and exposure to Fresh Graduates Engineers on Niche Technologies thereby reducing the “deployable time” for both the candidate, as well as the prospective employer.
It helps candidates attain stability between theoretical studies and realistic job exposure through hand-on expertise in Design/Developmental Skills, Requirement Analysis, Testing skills, Exposure to Standardization/QA etc.
Helps in enhancing professional skills among the candidates in various areas such as problem-solving abilities; communication skills; presentation skills, confidence enhancement, individual grooming, enterprise etiquettes, etc.
Perks for the candidates

* Completion Certificate
* Stipend- INR 10,000 per month
* Placement Assistance

Period of Programme- 6 Months (Next batch Commencing on- Jan/Feb 2023)

Some of the Key technologies that can be leveraged under the programme are:

Artificial Intelligence (AI) and Machine Learning
Robotic Process Automation (RPA)
Quantum Computing • Augmented Reality & Virtual Reality (AR/VR)
Block chain
Wireless Networks (5G, Wi-Fi 6 etc.)
Smart Mobility (Including Vehicular and Drone Technology)
Internet of Things (IOT)
Cyber Security and Cyber Forensics
Big Data Analytics
Digital Preservation
Cloud Computing
3D Printing
Flexible Electronics
Emerging Memory/ Storage Technologies
Machine vision (MV)
CPU Design
Area of work / activities in the organization can include specific / targeted project work, capability building initiatives, design-based activities, developmental activities, research-based activities, etc.

Individual will get the opportunity to work on Live Projects and Technologies.

WBL is facilitated through Seven (7) Organizations of MeitY i.e. CERT-IN, C-DAC, NIELIT, STQC, CMET, ERNET and SAMEER constituting of total 81 Centers or Units.

These opportunities are available on AICTE internship portal.

Internship Opportunities can be found here:
https://internship.aicte-india.org/ernet.php

It is requested to share this information among your student network and ask them to register on the portal and avail the benefits.

We hope that our internship portal, which is entirely free of cost, will be helpful to your students in adapting to a transparent internship process and abundant access to real, credible and the most genuine opportunities.

For any clarifications, feel free to contact us.

With Regards,
Dr. Buddha Chandrasekhar,

1/10/23, 11:33 - Prof. Dr Uday Patka(HOD): India International Science Festival (IISF) is a platform for public participation to inculcate scientific perspective and promote interest in science. Seven editions of IISF have been organized at various places across the country in the past. This year, eighth edition of IISF is being organized at Maulana Azad Naitonal Institute of Technology (MANIT), Bhopal, Madhya Pradesh. Theme for the 8th edition of IISF is Marching Towards Amrit Kaal with Science, Technology and Innovation.
             Students Innovation Festival (SIF) is an event of IISF where college level onwards students participate in competition and also showcase their talents on an international stage. The Themes of SIF-2022 are: Developing Sustainable Life based on Five Elements of Nature: The Earth, The Water, The fire, The air and The space. Students from engineering as well as science streams, who are interested and involved in innovation and creativity can participate in the Students’ Innovation Festival (SIF-2022).
            The selected models/entries will be showcased in the IISF on 22-23 January, 2023 at MANIT, Bhopal. Registration can be done on the website https://scienceindiafest.org . For detailed information, Brochure and Poster of SIF-2022 are enclosed herewith. The last date for registration by the students is 13th January, 2023.
            In this regard you are requested to encourage students at your institutions to be part of such endeavour towards innovation. Your cooperation will help the students of every corner of our country to have opportunity to participate in such an event of National importance.

Dear Sir / Ma'am,
Greetings from Maharashtra Association of Training & Placement Officers (MaTPO) and Government of Maharashtra’s Directorate of Technical Education (DTE)!!!
Great news: more than 25,400 students enrolled for MaTPO Aptitude Idol-2023 till date and the count is still going on...
Thanks to all TPOs across Maharashtra for their wholehearted support for enrolling their students in such a big numbers.
● College wise registration count (till 8th March 2023): 
https://tinyurl.com/MAI-23-Reg-8Mar 
We have received many requests from students through their TPOs for extending the deadline of student registration for MaTPO Aptitude Idol-2023. Hence we are extending the deadline for student registration to 10th March 2023, Friday till 10:00 AM.
Kindly encourage your maximum students to enroll at the earliest.
● Student Registration Link: https://tinyurl.com/MaTPO-Aptitude-Idol-2023
● Updated Last date to register: 10th March 2023, Friday till 10:00 AM
MaTPO in association with Government of Maharashtra’s DTE have organized "MaTPO Aptitude Idol-2023", an online aptitude competition for Maharashtra Students from First Year to Final Year of B.E. / B.Tech. / M.E. / M.Tech. / Diploma / BCA / MCA / BCS / MCS / BBA / MBA / B.Sc. / M.Sc. / B.Pharm. / M.Pharm. and other courses. Our objective is to improve the Employability of our Maharashtra students so that they can get more job offers.
● Date & Time of Round-1 (Online Aptitude Test): 11th March 2023, Saturday from 08:00 am to 07:00 pm
● Duration of this online aptitude test: 60 minutes
● Test Pattern & Syllabus for this online aptitude test: https://tinyurl.com/Syllabus-MaTPO-Apti-Idol-23 
● Venue: Your own college (request to TPOs / HODs / Class teachers / Other Concern people to make the necessary arrangements for the online aptitude test for your students in batches as per number of students)
We Request you to Make it Compulsory to all students so that Placement % / Internship % of your institute improves to a great extent. All Department HODs are requested to make arrangements for tests of their students.
Please share this information with students at the earliest & ask them to prepare properly to get expected output.
● Who can participate?: Students from any college across Maharashtra from First Year to Final Year of B.E. / B.Tech. / M.E. / M.Tech. / Diploma / BCA / MCA / BCS / MCS / BBA / MBA / B.Sc. / M.Sc. / B.Pharm. / M.Pharm. and other courses
● Win exciting Prizes: Laptop, Mobile, Tab, Fitbit, Bag, etc.
● VERY IMPORTANT NOTE:
1. Students will receive all the necessary guidelines to appear for this online aptitude test on 10th March 2023 @4:00pm through live streaming on our FaceBook Page: https://www.facebook.com/ConnectMaTPO. It is compulsory for all the students to attend this guidance session.
2. No charges are applicable to participate.

● About MaTPO: 
▪︎ MaTPO is an association of around 500 Training & Placement Officers of Engineering, Diploma, MBA, BBA, MCA, BCA, M.Sc., B.Sc., MCS, BCS, M.Pharm., B.Pharm. and other courses from across Maharashtra. 
▪︎ We conduct many employment related activities like Pool Campus Recruitment Drives, Job Fairs, Apprenticeship Fairs, etc. We also arrange Industry Institute Interaction Meets, Expert sessions by Industry Professionals, Aptitude Contests, Programming Contests, etc. to enhance the employability of our Maharashtra students. *Computational Intelligence (CI)* is the theory, design, application and development of biologically and linguistically motivated computational paradigms. Traditionally the three main pillars of CI have been  *Neural Networks, Fuzzy Systems and Evolutionary Computation*. CI is an evolving field that encompasses computing paradigms like ambient intelligence, artificial life, cultural learning, artificial endocrine networks, social reasoning, and artificial hormone networks. 
Join the webinar to learn more about *State-of-art in Computational Intelligence*!

3/13/23, 21:58 - Prof. Dr Uday Patka(HOD): 🔖Programming Contest for students of First Year to Final Year: "MaTPO PROGRAMMING IDOL-2023", an online coding competition organized by Maharashtra Association of Training & Placement Officers (MaTPO) in association with Govt. of Maharashtra's Directorate of Technical Education (DTE), Geeks for Geeks (GFG) and NASSCOM on Saturday, 18th March 2023 II 3 categories as per year of passing (Final Year, Pre Final Year & First / Second Year) || Question papers & time slots for 3 categories are different || Test Pattern & Syllabus is attached || Programming Languages options : C++, Java & Python || Test can be given from Home / College || Last Date to register: 15th March 2023 till 04:00 pm🔖

Dear Sir / Ma’am,

Greetings from DTE Maharashtra, MaTPO, GFG & NASSCOM FutureSkills Prime!!!

After a huge response of 34,767 students who have enrolled for MaTPO Aptitude Idol-2023, now we are coming up with MaTPO Programming Idol-2023. We are happy to share with you that MaTPO in association with DTE Maharashtra, GFG & NASSCOM FutureSkills Prime has organized "MaTPO Programming Idol-2023", an online coding competition. Our objective is to improve the Employability of our Maharashtra students so that they can get more job offers.

● Date & Time of Round-1 (Online Coding Test): 18th March 2023, Saturday in 3 Categories as follows:
(Question paper & time slot for each category is different. Hence students must appear in the category allotted to particular year like Final year / Pre Final year / First & Second year for UG / PG / Diploma)
▪︎Category 1 – Final year – UG/PG – 10:00 am to 12:00 pm 
▪︎Category 2 – Pre Final year – UG/PG – 12:30 pm to 02:30 pm 
▪︎Category 3 – First & Second year – UG/Diploma – 03:00 pm to 05:00 pm

● Venue: Student can give the test from Home or College

● Duration: 2 hrs 

● Student Registration Link: https://tinyurl.com/MPI-23-Reg 

● Last date to register: 15th March 2023, Wednesday till 04:00 pm

● Test Pattern & Syllabus:
1. The coding contest consists of a total 3 coding-based situational Data Structure & Algorithms (DSA) questions in each category.
2. Languages supported for the contest are C++, Java and Python.
3. Any type of Plagiarism will not be entertained. If anyone is caught doing that the score of the concerned participant will get 0. 

● Test Pattern & Syllabus: https://tinyurl.com/Syllabus-MPI-23 

We request you to encourage all students to participate so that Placement % & Internship % of our Maharashtra students improves to a great extent.

Please share this information with students at the earliest so that they can prepare for 5-6 days to get expected output.

● Who can participate?: Students from any college across Maharashtra from First Year to Final Year of B.E. / B.Tech. / M.E. / M.Tech. / Diploma / BCA / MCA / BCS / MCS / BBA / MBA / B.Sc. / M.Sc. / B.Pharm. / M.Pharm. and other courses

● Separate winners & prizes will be there for all categories: Laptop, Mobile, Tab, Fitbit, Bag, etc.

● IMPORTANT NOTE:
1. While filling this Google form, please enter your Email ID correctly (do not make any spelling mistake) as all further communication will be done through email only. Even the Test Link will be shared on the same email ID.
2. You will receive all the necessary guidelines to appear for this online programming test on 17th March 2023 @4:00pm through live streaming on our FaceBook Page: https://www.facebook.com/ConnectMaTPO. It is compulsory for all the students to attend this guidance session.
3. No charges are applicable to participate.
